		<!-- betslip interation -->
		<script type="text/javascript">
			// betslip interaction class

				var betSLipInteraction = function() {
				if($('#betSlipContainer').length)
				{
					this.animate();
				}
			};
			// already in interaction
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.stop					= false;
			// frames per second to check
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.framesPerSecond 		= 1;
			// content height
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.contentHeight 			= 0;
			// left column height
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.columnHeight 			= 0;
			// window possition at this moment
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.currentWindowPosition 	= 0;
			// height of the header
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.headerHeight 			= 0;
			// height of the leagues widget
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.widgetHeight 			= 0;
			// position to animate to
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.animateTo 				= 0;
			// hadler of the animation
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.animateHandler			= false;
			// hadler of the timouts
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.timeoutHandler			= false;
			// animate
			betSLipInteraction.prototype.animate 				= function()
			{
				// basic setup
				// instance to be passed for the lamda functions

				var instance 	= this;
				this.columnHeight 	= isNaN(Number($("#leftColumn").height())) 	 ? 0 : $("#leftColumn").height() + $("#my-bets-source").height();
				this.headerHeight 	= $('#header').height();
				this.contentHeight 	= isNaN(Number($("#mainContent").height()))  ? 0 : Number($("#mainContent").height());

				// when betslip is not in motion
				if(
						false == this.stop
					&&	this.contentHeight > this.columnHeight
				)
				{
					this.stop = true;
					// basic settlement
					this.currentWindowPosition = isNaN(Number($(window).scrollTop())) ? 0 : Number($(window).scrollTop());

					if($('#topWidgets').length)
					{
						this.widgetHeight 			= isNaN(parseInt($('#topWidgets').css('height'))) ? 0 : parseInt($('#topWidgets').css('height'));
					}

					// animate to calculus and logic
					var	leftColumnHeightTotalValue = $('#leftColumn').height(),
						leftColumnCurrentTopOffset = $('#leftColumn').offset().top,
						leftColumnFromTop = leftColumnHeightTotalValue + leftColumnCurrentTopOffset - 110;

					this.animateTo = parseInt(this.currentWindowPosition - this.headerHeight - this.widgetHeight);

					this.animateTo =
					(
						this.animateTo >= 0 ?
						(
							(this.animateTo + leftColumnHeightTotalValue) >= this.contentHeight ?
							(
							//this.contentHeight - this.columnHeight
							this.contentHeight - leftColumnHeightTotalValue
							//this.currentWindowPosition - this.headerHeight - this.widgetHeight
							)
							:
							this.currentWindowPosition - this.headerHeight - this.widgetHeight
						) 	:
							0
					);

					if (0 != this.animateTo)
					{
						$('#leftColumn').css({"margin-top": this.animateTo - 10+ "px"});
						$('.enscroll-track-wrapper').css({"margin-top": this.animateTo - 10 + "px"});

					}

					else
					{
						$('#leftColumn').css({"marginTop": "0px"});
						$('.enscroll-track-wrapper').css({"marginTop": "0px"});
					}
				//Left Column Scroll Height
					var fullScreenHeight = $(window).height(),
						lcHeight = fullScreenHeight - 129;
						if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 110) {
							lcHeight = fullScreenHeight - 20;
						}
						$('#leftColumn').css('height', lcHeight+'px');


					this.stop = false;
				}
				else
				{
					$('#leftColumn').css({"marginTop": "0px"});
                    $('.enscroll-track-wrapper').css({"marginTop": "0px"});
				}

				// animation handler
				if(false == this.animateHandler)
				{
					$(window).scroll(function(){instance.animate();});
					this.animateHandler = true;
				}
				if(false != this.timeoutHandler)
				{
					clearTimeout(this.timeoutHandler);
				}
				this.timeoutHandler = setTimeout(function(){instance.animate()}, 1000/instance.framesPerSecond)
			};
			$('#runningBetsTabInMyBets, .statusBets').on('click', function(){
				betSLipInteraction.prototype.animate;
			});

			$(function(){new betSLipInteraction();});

$(document).ready(function(){
	/* EnScroll
	*******************/
				$('#leftColumn').enscroll({
					verticalTrackClass: 'track1',
					verticalHandleClass: 'handle1',
					drawScrollButtons: true,
					scrollUpButtonClass: 'scroll-up',
					scrollDownButtonClass: 'scroll-down'
				});
				$('#leftColumn').on('mouseenter', function(){
					$('#leftColumn').addClass('scrollable');

					// Turn off the scroll
					$(document).on('wheel', '.scrollable', function(evt) {
						var offsetTop = this.scrollTop + parseInt(evt.originalEvent.deltaY, 10);
						var offsetBottom = this.scrollHeight - this.getBoundingClientRect().height - offsetTop;

						if (offsetTop < 0 || offsetBottom < 0) {
							evt.preventDefault();
						} else {
							evt.stopImmediatePropagation();
						}
					});
	})
	/* OPEN TICKERS
	*******************/
	if($('.ticker-item').length > 0)
	{
		$('.tickers').click();
				}

	/* BETLIST
	*******************/
		betListHeb();

	/* CASINO HEB GAMES NAMES
	**************************/
			// if (Config.LOCALE == 'iw_IL'){
			// 	$('.game_title').each(function(){
			// 		var $div = $(this);
			// 		var divWords = $div.html().split(/\s+/);

			// 		$div.empty();

			// 		$.each(divWords, function(i,w){
			// 			$('<span/>').html(w).appendTo($div);
			// 		});

			// 		$(this).find($('span')).each(function(){
			// 			var cat = $(this).width();
			// 			cat = cat + $(this).width();
			// 			console.info(cat)})
			// 	})
			// }

	/* MIN PAGE Height
	*******************/

	var fixedLayoutMinHeight = $(window).height() - 200;
		$('#mainContent').css('min-height', fixedLayoutMinHeight + 'px');
		if (window.location.href.indexOf('sport/index')<=0 && window.location.href.indexOf('multi-view') == -1){
			$('.sport-table').css('min-height', fixedLayoutMinHeight + 'px');
				}
		$('.cms-container, .main-content-container, .cards_container').css('min-height', fixedLayoutMinHeight + 'px');
});

   function betListHeb(parent) {
	   if (!parent)
	   {
		   parent = $(document);
	   }
				if (parent.find('.bet_type strong').length >= 1 && Config.LOCALE == 'iw_IL'){

					parent.find('.bet_type strong, .bet_type strong span, .cell.item_content').each(function(){
						var $div = $(this);
						var divWords = $div.html().split(/\s+/);

						$div.empty();


						$.each(divWords, function(i,w){
							$('<span/>').html(w).appendTo($div);
						});
					})

					parent.find('.item_content.rtl_control, .row_id_content .description_content .description, .cell.selection strong, .cell.selection strong span').each(function(){
									var $div = $(this);
									var divWords = $div.text().split(/\s+/);

									$div.empty();


									$.each(divWords, function(i,w){
										$('<span/>').text(w).appendTo($div);
									});
					})

				parent.find('.bet_type strong, .description, .cell.selection strong, .bet_type strong span').each(function(){
						// console.warn($(this).find('span').length);
						if ($(this).find('span').length == 3 && $(this).find('span:empty').length == 2 ){
							$(this).find('span').addClass('correct_score_item');
						}
				})

			}
		};

		$(function(){
			$('.blink-preloader').remove();
		})
